[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Fix Strategy[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. Root Cause Identification[0m                                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - The infinite hang occurs in [0m[1;35mType1Parser.parseBinary[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m at the loop that skips [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mtokens until the [0m[32m"/CharStrings"[0m[39m literal is found:[0m                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     ```[0m                                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     while [0m[1;39m([0m[39m![0m[1;39m([0m[1;35mlexer.peekKind[0m[1;39m([0m[39mToken.LITERAL[0m[1;39m)[0m                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m             && [0m[1;35mlexer.peekToken[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[1;35m.getText[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[1;35m.equals[0m[1;39m([0m[32m"CharStrings"[0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     [0m[1;39m{[0m                                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m         [0m[1;35mlexer.nextToken[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     [0m[1;39m}[0m                                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     ```[0m                                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     If the input is malformed or adversarial [0m[1;39m([0m[39mmissing [0m[32m"CharStrings"[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m, [0m             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`[0m[1;35mpeekToken[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` eventually returns null but `[0m[1;35mpeekKind[0m[1;39m([0m[33m...[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` remains false, so the [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mloop never exits—causing an infinite loop and resulting timeout.[0m                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. Patch Location[0m                                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - File: fontbox/src/main/java/org/apache/fontbox/type1/Type1Parser.java[0m          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Method: private void [0m[1;35mparseBinary[0m[1;39m([0m[39mbyte[0m[1;39m[[0m[1;39m][0m[39m bytes[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m throws IOException[0m              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Lines to modify: around [0m[1;36m640[0m[39m–[0m[1;36m645[0m[39m [0m[1;39m([0m[39mthe skipping-loop for [0m[32m"/CharStrings"[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m.[0m        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3[0m[39m. Detailed Patch Steps[0m                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   a. Replace the existing loop with a null-safe variant that:[0m                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      - Peeks the next token.[0m                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      - If token is null [0m[1;39m([0m[39mEOF[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m, throws an IOException to abort parsing.[0m             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      - If token matches the literal [0m[32m"CharStrings"[0m[39m, breaks out of the loop.[0m         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      - Otherwise, consumes the token and continues.[0m                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   b. Concrete replacement logic:[0m                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      ```java[0m                                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      [0m[35m/[0m[35m/[0m[39m Skip until [0m[35m/[0m[95mCharStrings[0m[39m literal or EOF[0m                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      Token token = [0m[1;35mlexer.peekToken[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      while [0m[1;39m([0m[39mtoken != null[0m                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m             && ![0m[1;39m([0m[1;35mtoken.getKind[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m == Token.LITERAL[0m                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m                  && [0m[32m"CharStrings"[0m[1;35m.equals[0m[1;39m([0m[1;35mtoken.getText[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      [0m[1;39m{[0m                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m          [0m[1;35mlexer.nextToken[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m          token = [0m[1;35mlexer.peekToken[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      [0m[1;39m}[0m                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      if [0m[1;39m([0m[39mtoken == null[0m[1;39m)[0m                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      [0m[1;39m{[0m                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m          throw new [0m[1;35mIOException[0m[1;39m([0m[32m"/CharStrings token not found"[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      [0m[1;39m}[0m                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      [0m[35m/[0m[35m/[0m[39m At this point, token is the [0m[32m"CharStrings"[0m[39m literal[0m                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      ```[0m                                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   c. Leave the subsequent `[0m[1;35mread[0m[1;39m([0m[39mToken.LITERAL, [0m[32m"CharStrings"[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;` and [0m               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`[0m[1;35mreadCharStrings[0m[1;39m([0m[39mlenIV[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;` calls intact, ensuring correct behavior on well-formed [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mfonts.[0m                                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m4[0m[39m. Additional Hardening [0m[1;39m([0m[39mOptional but Recommended[0m[1;39m)[0m                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - To guard against resource-exhaustion via oversized binary segments, insert a [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39msanity check at the start of `parseBinary`:[0m                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     ```java[0m                                                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     private static final int MAX_BINARY_LENGTH = 50_000_000; [0m[35m/[0m[35m/[0m[39m e.g. 50MB[0m          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     private void [0m[1;35mparseBinary[0m[1;39m([0m[39mbyte[0m[1;39m[[0m[1;39m][0m[39m bytes[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m throws IOException[0m                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     [0m[1;39m{[0m                                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m         if [0m[1;39m([0m[39mbytes.length > MAX_BINARY_LENGTH[0m[1;39m)[0m                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m         [0m[1;39m{[0m                                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m             throw new [0m[1;35mIOException[0m[1;39m([0m[32m"Binary segment too large: "[0m[39m + bytes.length[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m         [0m[1;39m}[0m                                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m         [0m[35m/[0m[35m/[0m[39m existing decryption and parsing logic follows[0m[33m...[0m                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     [0m[1;39m}[0m                                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     ```[0m                                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Choose the threshold based on realistic maximum Type [0m[1;36m1[0m[39m font sizes in PDF [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mcontexts. This preempts excessive work/decryption loops on extremely large inputs.[0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m5[0m[39m. Preservation of Functionality[0m                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Well-formed PFB fonts that contain the [0m[32m"/CharStrings"[0m[39m dictionary are [0m          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39munaffected; parsing proceeds normally.[0m                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - The exception path only triggers on malformed or malicious inputs that would [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39motherwise hang, converting a hang into a fast failure.[0m                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Existing unit tests and PDFTextStripper behavior remain unchanged for valid [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mfonts.[0m                                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m6[0m[39m. Side Effects and Mitigations[0m                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Malformed fonts will now produce an IOException instead of hanging; this is [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39macceptable as the fonts were already non-conformant.[0m                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - The optional size check may reject unusually large but valid fonts—mitigate by[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mtuning `MAX_BINARY_LENGTH` to cover legitimate use cases or making it configurable.[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - No changes are made to harness, fuzzing code, or external libraries. All [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mmodifications are localized to Type1Parser.[0m                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m7[0m[39m. Justification[0m                                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Introducing an EOF/null check in the skip loop directly addresses the infinite[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mloop root cause.[0m                                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Fail-fast on missing tokens prevents denial-of-service timeouts under fuzzing.[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - This approach mirrors similar defensive patterns elsewhere in FontBox [0m[1;39m([0m[39me.g., [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mthrowing on missing [0m[32m"/Private"[0m[39m tokens[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m and keeps the parser robust yet forgiving [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mfor valid data.[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<[0m[35m/[0m[95mfix_strategy[0m[1m>[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         ===Evaluation [33mEnd[0m===                                                                [2m                [0m
